<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a> (75800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gemahl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">gemahele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gimahalo</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gemahela</i>, which didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> persist into Middle Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaals</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemalen.html>gemalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemaal.html>gemaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemalin.html>gemalin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in titles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A consort.</li>
<li>A husband.</li></ol>

***gemeengoed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeengoed.html>gemeengoed</a> (93140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Early 19th century. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gemeingut</i> but perhaps also influenced by earlier use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> as a set phrase.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeengoed.html>gemeengoed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeengoed.html>gemeengoederen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>common property</li>
<li>common practice, common feature

***gemeente.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a> (6212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gemeende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gimēnitha</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamainiz</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-iþō</i>. Corresponds to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenten.html>gemeenten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeentes.html>gemeentes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeentetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>municipality, commune</li>
<li>congregation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the Netherlands and Belgium, a municipality (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeente.html>gemeente</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> part of a province (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a></i>), and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> analogous to a county. Villages and small <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>towns</a> in a municipality are called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dorpen.html>dorpen</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaatsen.html>plaatsen</a></i>. Larger <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>towns</a> and cities are called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>steden</a></i>.
</p>

<p>Form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">common</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i> (superlative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

***gemoed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemoed.html>gemoed</a> (32644)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghemoede</i>. Analyzable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moed.html>moed</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gemüt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gemēde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemoed.html>gemoed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemoederen.html>gemoederen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemoed.html>gemoedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>feeling; heart; soul; mind</li></ol>

***gemoeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemoeten.html>gemoeten</a> (14748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemoeten.html>gemoeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gimuoten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamōtijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gemoeten.html>gemoeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to meet, to encounter</li></ol>

***genadeloos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a> (16685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genade.html>genade</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mercy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadelozer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">genadeloost</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of persons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> merciless, ruthless; heartless
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strenge.html>strenge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leraar.html>leraar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a></b>: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a> per <a href = vnd.unilang:fout.html>fout</a></i>
<dl><dd>The strict teacher <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> merciless: a point per error</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> merciless, unforgiving, harsh</li></ol>
